<td>1

<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque_style" title="Category:Baroque style">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td><i>Voices</i>: 2 haut-dessus, haute-contre, taille, basse + mixed chorus (SATB)<br /><i>Orchestra</i>: 2 flutes, 2 oboes + 2 trumpets + drums + strings (4) + continuo
</td></tr>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<ul><li> According to Grove, the only Te Deum with trumpets is H.146 in D. <br />
</li><li> The prelude is known as "Eurovision hymn" ("Eurovisionsmelodie")
</li></ul>
